Connect the client to the service \hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_aad7fa3b34d9d72a2f1d4baa681ba25cc}{}\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Create@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Create}}

Create a new e\+Call object

The e\+Call is not actually established at this point. It\textquotesingle{}s still up to the caller to call le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Start() when ready.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A reference to the new Call object.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
On failure, the process exits; you don\textquotesingle{}t have to worry about checking the returned reference for validity. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\subsubsection[{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{le__ecall__interface_8h_a924114fa7fab10c3f351766a76134f34}
This function exits from e\+Call Only mode. It configures the e\+Call operation mode to Normal mode, the modem uses the default operation mode at power up (or after U/\+S\+I\+M hotswap). The modem behaves following the U/\+S\+I\+M e\+Call operation mode; for example the U/\+S\+I\+M can be configured only for e\+Call, or a combination of e\+Call and commercial service provision.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+K on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T for other failures 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_aebdb7744c37081fda6398031d3ee1198}{}\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Export\+Msd@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Export\+Msd}}

Export the encoded M\+S\+D.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+N\+D No encoded M\+S\+D is available.

\hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_a042d52c84b5b679ab32dd814c5b0be9e}{}\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode}}
\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{le__ecall__interface_8h_a042d52c84b5b679ab32dd814c5b0be9e}
This function configures the e\+Call operation mode to e\+Call only, only emergency number can be used to start an e\+Call session. The modem doesn\textquotesingle{}t try to register on the Cellular network. This function forces the modem to behave as e\+Call only mode whatever U/\+S\+I\+M operation mode. The change doesn\textquotesingle{}t persist over power cycles. This function can be called before making an e\+Call.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+K on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T for other failures 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

M\+S\+D is transmitted only after an emergency call has been established.

\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T for other failures
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Set tthe A\+U\+T\+O\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+E\+M\+P\+T\+S value. If a dial attempt under automatic emergency call initiation failed, it should be repeated maximally E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+E\+M\+P\+T\+S-\/1 times within the maximal time limit of E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+U\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N. The default value is 10. Redial attempts stop once the call has been cleared down correctly, or if counter/timer reached their limits.

Set the E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+U\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N time. It\textquotesingle{}s the maximum time the I\+V\+S have to connect the emergency call to the P\+S\+A\+P, including all redial attempts. If the call is not connected within this time (or Manual\+Dial\+Attempts/\+Auto\+Dial\+Attempts dial attempts), it will stop.
